<h3 id="221-serverproperties" style='font-family:"microsoft yahei"; font-weight:100; line-height:1.1; color:rgb(63,63,63); margin:0.8em 0px; font-size:1.7em; padding:0px'>
<a target="_blank" name="t4" style="background:transparent; color:rgb(79,161,219); margin:0px; padding:0px; outline:0px"></a>2.2.1 server.properties</h3>
<p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:1.7em; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; line-height:27.2px; word-wrap:break-word; word-break:normal; color:rgb(63,63,63); font-family:"microsoft yahei"; font-size:16px'>
只设置了以下4项，其他使用默认值</p>
<pre class="prettyprint" style='font-family:"Source Code Pro",monospace; font-size:14px; white-space:nowrap; padding:5px 5px 5px 60px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:1.7em; line-height:23.8px; color:rgb(51,51,51); word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; position:relative; overflow-y:hidden; overflow-x:auto'><code class="language-bash hljs  has-numbering" style='font-family:"Source Code Pro",monospace; font-size:12.6px; padding:0px; color:inherit; white-space:pre; background:transparent; display:block; overflow-x:auto; word-wrap:normal'><span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)"># 当前机器在集群中的唯一标识，和zookeeper的myid性质一样</span>
broker.id=<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">0</span>

host.name=hsm01

<span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)"># 消息存放的目录，这个目录可以配置为“，”逗号分割的表达式，</span>
<span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)"># 上面的num.io.threads要大于这个目录的个数这个目录，如果配置多个目录，</span>
<span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)"># 新创建的topic他把消息持久化的地方是，当前以逗号分割的目录中，</span>
<span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)"># 那个分区数最少就放那一个</span>
log.dirs=/home/zkpk/kafka_2.<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">11</span>-<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">0.9</span>.<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">0.1</span>/logs

<span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)"># 配置自定义的ZooKeeper</span>
zookeeper.connect=hsm01:<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">2181</span>,hss01:<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">2181</span>,hss02:<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">2181</span>/kafka</code></pre><ul class="pre-numbering" style="margin:0px; padding:6px 0px 40px; list-style:none; line-height:23.8px; position:absolute; width:50px; background-color:rgb(238,238,238); top:0px; left:0px; border-right:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); text-align:right"><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">1</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">2</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">3</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">4</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">5</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">6</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">7</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">8</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">9</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">10</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">11</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">12</li><li style="margin:0px; padding:0px 5px; list-style:none; color:rgb(153,153,153)">13</li></ul>

注意storm-core依赖的scope <br style="">

<h3 id="422-helloworldspoutjava" style='font-family:"microsoft yahei"; font-weight:100; line-height:1.1; color:rgb(63,63,63); margin:0.8em 0px; font-size:1.7em; padding:0px'>
<a target="_blank" name="t21" style="background:transparent; color:rgb(79,161,219); margin:0px; padding:0px; outline:0px"></a>4.2.2 HelloWorldSpout.java</h3>
<pre class="prettyprint" style='font-family:"Source Code Pro",monospace; font-size:14px; white-space:nowrap; padding:5px 5px 5px 60px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:1.7em; line-height:23.8px; color:rgb(51,51,51); word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; position:relative; overflow-y:hidden; overflow-x:auto'><code class="hljs java has-numbering" style='font-family:"Source Code Pro",monospace; font-size:12.6px; padding:0px; color:inherit; white-space:pre; background:transparent; display:block; overflow-x:auto; word-wrap:normal'><span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">package</span> com.zw.storm.helloworld;

<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.spout.SpoutOutputCollector;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.task.TopologyContext;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.topology.OutputFieldsDeclarer;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.topology.base.BaseRichSpout;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.tuple.Fields;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.tuple.Values;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.utils.Utils;

<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> java.util.Map;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> java.util.Random;

<span class="hljs-javadoc" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">/**
 * Spout起到和外界沟通的作用，他可以从一个数据库中按照某种规则取数据，也可以从分布式队列中取任务
 * &lt;p&gt;
 *     生成一个随机数生成的Tuple
 * &lt;/p&gt;
 *
 * Created by zhangws on 16/10/3.
 */</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-class" style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">class</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)">HelloWorldSpout</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)">BaseRichSpout</span> {</span>

    <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// 用来发射数据的工具类</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">private</span> SpoutOutputCollector collector;

    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">int</span> referenceRandom;

    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">final</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">int</span> MAX_RANDOM = <span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">10</span>;

    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px">HelloWorldSpout</span>() {
        <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">final</span> Random rand = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> Random();
        referenceRandom = rand.nextInt(MAX_RANDOM);
    }

    <span class="hljs-javadoc" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">/**
     * 定义字段id，该id在简单模式下没有用处，但在按照字段分组的模式下有很大的用处。
     * &lt;p&gt;
     *     该declarer变量有很大作用，我们还可以调用declarer.declareStream();
     *     来定义stramId，该id可以用来定义更加复杂的流拓扑结构
     * &lt;/p&gt;
     *<span class="hljs-javadoctag" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)"> @param</span> outputFieldsDeclarer
     */</span>
    <span class="hljs-annotation" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(155,133,157)">@Override</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">void</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px">declareOutputFields</span>(OutputFieldsDeclarer outputFieldsDeclarer) {
        outputFieldsDeclarer.declare(<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> Fields(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"sentence"</span>));
    }

    <span class="hljs-javadoc" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">/**
     * 初始化collector
     *
     *<span class="hljs-javadoctag" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)"> @param</span> map
     *<span class="hljs-javadoctag" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)"> @param</span> topologyContext
     *<span class="hljs-javadoctag" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)"> @param</span> spoutOutputCollector
     */</span>
    <span class="hljs-annotation" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(155,133,157)">@Override</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">void</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px">open</span>(Map map, TopologyContext topologyContext,
                     SpoutOutputCollector spoutOutputCollector) {
        <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">this</span>.collector = spoutOutputCollector;
    }

    <span class="hljs-javadoc" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">/**
     * 每调用一次就可以向storm集群中发射一条数据（一个tuple元组），该方法会被不停的调用
     */</span>
    <span class="hljs-annotation" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(155,133,157)">@Override</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">void</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px">nextTuple</span>() {
        Utils.sleep(<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">100</span>);
        <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">final</span> Random rand = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> Random();
        <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">int</span> instanceRandom = rand.nextInt(MAX_RANDOM);
        <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">if</span> (instanceRandom == referenceRandom) {
            collector.emit(<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> Values(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"Hello World"</span>));
        } <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">else</span> {
            collector.emit(<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> Values(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"Other Random Word"</span>));
        }
    }
}</code></pre><ul class="pre-numbering" style="margin:0px; padding:6px 0px 40px; list-style:none; line-height:23.8px; position:absolute; width:50px; background-color:rgb(238,238,238); top:0px; left:0px; <a target="_blank" name="t23" style="background:transparent; color:rgb(79,161,219); margin:0px; padding:0px; outline:0px"></a>4.2.4 HelloWorldTopology.java</h3>
<pre class="prettyprint" style='font-family:"Source Code Pro",monospace; font-size:14px; white-space:nowrap; padding:5px 5px 5px 60px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:1.7em; line-height:23.8px; color:rgb(51,51,51); word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; position:relative; overflow-y:hidden; overflow-x:auto'><code class="hljs java has-numbering" style='font-family:"Source Code Pro",monospace; font-size:12.6px; padding:0px; color:inherit; white-space:pre; background:transparent; display:block; overflow-x:auto; word-wrap:normal'><span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">package</span> com.zw.storm.helloworld;

<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.Config;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.LocalCluster;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.StormSubmitter;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.topology.TopologyBuilder;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.utils.Utils;

<span class="hljs-javadoc" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">/**
 * mvn compile exec:java -Dexec.classpathScope=compile -Dexec.mainClass=com.zw.storm.helloworld.HelloWorldTopology
 * Created by zhangws on 16/10/4.
 */</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-class" style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">class</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)">HelloWorldTopology</span> {</span>

    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">void</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px">main</span>(String[] args) <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">throws</span> Exception {
        TopologyBuilder builder = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> TopologyBuilder();
        <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// 设置喷发节点并分配并发数，该并发数将会控制该对象在集群中的线程数。</span>
        builder.setSpout(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"randomHelloWorld"</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> HelloWorldSpout(), <span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">1</span>);
        <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// 设置数据处理节点并分配并发数。指定该节点接收喷发节点的策略为随机方式。</span>
        builder.setBolt(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"HelloWorldBolt"</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> HelloWorldBolt(), <span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">2</span>)
                .shuffleGrouping(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"randomHelloWorld"</span>);

        Config config = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> Config();
        config.setDebug(<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">true</span>);

        <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">if</span> (args != <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">null</span> &amp;&amp; args.length &gt; <span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">0</span>) {
            config.setNumWorkers(<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">1</span>);
            StormSubmitter.submitTopology(args[<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">0</span>], config, builder.createTopology());
        } <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">else</span> {
            <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// 这里是本地模式下运行的启动代码。</span>
            config.setMaxTaskParallelism(<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">1</span>);
            LocalCluster cluster = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> LocalCluster();
            cluster.submitTopology(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"test"</span>, config, builder.createTopology());
            Utils.sleep(<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">10000</span>);
            cluster.killTopology(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"test"</span>);
            cluster.shutdown();
        }
    }

<h3 id="425-运行" style='font-family:"microsoft yahei"; font-weight:100; line-height:1.1; color:rgb(63,63,63); margin:0.8em 0px; font-size:1.7em; padding:0px'>
<a target="_blank" name="t24" style="background:transparent; color:rgb(79,161,219); margin:0px; padding:0px; outline:0px"></a>4.2.5 运行</h3>

<h3 id="432-messageschemejava" style='font-family:"microsoft yahei"; font-weight:100; line-height:1.1; color:rgb(63,63,63); margin:0.8em 0px; font-size:1.7em; padding:0px'>
<a target="_blank" name="t27" style="background:transparent; color:rgb(79,161,219); margin:0px; padding:0px; outline:0px"></a>4.3.2 MessageScheme.java</h3>
<pre class="prettyprint" style='font-family:"Source Code Pro",monospace; font-size:14px; white-space:nowrap; padding:5px 5px 5px 60px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:1.7em; line-height:23.8px; color:rgb(51,51,51); word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; position:relative; overflow-y:hidden; overflow-x:auto'><code class="hljs java has-numbering" style='font-family:"Source Code Pro",monospace; font-size:12.6px; padding:0px; color:inherit; white-space:pre; background:transparent; display:block; overflow-x:auto; word-wrap:normal'><span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">package</span> com.zw.kafka.storm;

<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.spout.Scheme;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.tuple.Fields;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> backtype.storm.tuple.Values;

<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> java.io.UnsupportedEncodingException;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> java.util.List;

<span class="hljs-javadoc" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">/**
 * 对kafka出来的数据转换成字符串
 * &lt;p&gt;
 *     KafkaSpout是Storm中自带的Spout,
 *     使用KafkaSpout时需要子集实现Scheme接口，它主要负责从消息流中解析出需要的数据
 * &lt;/p&gt;
 *
 * Created by zhangws on 16/10/2.
 */</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-class" style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">class</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)">MessageScheme</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)">Scheme</span> {</span>

    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> List&lt;Object&gt; <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px">deserialize</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">byte</span>[] bytes) {
        <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">try</span> {
            String msg = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> String(bytes, <span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"UTF-8"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">return</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> Values(msg);
        } <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">catch</span> (UnsupportedEncodingException e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
        <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">return</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">null</span>;
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> Fields <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px">getOutputFields</span>() {

<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-class" style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">class</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)">SequenceBolt</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)">BaseBasicBolt</span> {</span>

    <span class="hljs-javadoc" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">/**
     * Process the input tuple and optionally emit new tuples based on the input tuple.
     * &lt;p&gt;
     * All acking is managed for you. Throw a FailedException if you want to fail the tuple.
     *
     *<span class="hljs-javadoctag" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)"> @param</span> input
     *<span class="hljs-javadoctag" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)"> @param</span> collector
     */</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">void</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px">execute</span>(Tuple input, BasicOutputCollector collector) {
        String word = (String) input.getValue(<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">0</span>);
        System.out.println(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"=============="</span> + word);

        <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">//写文件</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">try</span> {
            DataOutputStream out_file = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> DataOutputStream(<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> FileOutputStream(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"/home/zkpk/kafkastorm.out"</span>));
            out_file.writeUTF(word);
            out_file.close();
        } <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">catch</span> (FileNotFoundException e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        } <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">catch</span> (IOException e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }

        collector.emit(<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> Values(word));
    }

    <span class="hljs-javadoc" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">/**

<a target="_blank" name="t29" style="background:transparent; color:rgb(79,161,219); margin:0px; padding:0px; outline:0px"></a>4.3.4 KafkaTopology.java</h3>
<pre class="prettyprint" style='font-family:"Source Code Pro",monospace; font-size:14px; white-space:nowrap; padding:5px 5px 5px 60px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:1.7em; line-height:23.8px; color:rgb(51,51,51); word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; position:relative; overflow-y:hidden; overflow-x:auto'><code class="hljs java has-numbering" style='font-family:"Source Code Pro",monospace; font-size:12.6px; padding:0px; color:inherit; white-space:pre; background:transparent; display:block; overflow-x:auto; word-wrap:normal'><span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">package</span> com.zw.kafka.storm;

<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> java.util.HashMap;
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">import</span> java.util.Map;

<span class="hljs-javadoc" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">/**
 * 配置kafka提交topology到storm的代码
 * &lt;p&gt;
 * topic1的含义kafka接收生产者过来的数据所需要的topic;
 * topic2是KafkaBolt也就是storm中的bolt生成的topic，当然这里topic2这行配置可以省略，
 * 是没有任何问题的，类似于一个中转的东西
 * &lt;/p&gt;
 * Created by zhangws on 16/10/2.
 */</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-class" style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">class</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(102,0,102)">KafkaTopology</span> {</span>

    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">final</span> String BROKER_ZK_LIST = <span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"hsm01:2181,hss01:2181,hss02:2181"</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">final</span> String ZK_PATH = <span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"/kafka/brokers"</span>;

    <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">void</span> <span class="hljs-title" style="margin:0px; padding:0px">main</span>(String[] args) <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">throws</span> Exception {
        <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// 配置Zookeeper地址</span>
        BrokerHosts brokerHosts = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> ZkHosts(BROKER_ZK_LIST, ZK_PATH);
        <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// 配置Kafka订阅的Topic，以及zookeeper中数据节点目录和名字</span>
        SpoutConfig spoutConfig = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> SpoutConfig(brokerHosts, <span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"sogolog"</span>, <span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"/kafka"</span>, <span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"kafka"</span>);

        <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// 配置KafkaBolt中的kafka.broker.properties</span>
        Config conf = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> Config();
        Map&lt;String, String&gt; map = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> HashMap&lt;String, String&gt;();

        <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// 配置Kafka broker地址</span>
        map.put(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"metadata.broker.list"</span>, <span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"hsm01:9092"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// serializer.class为消息的序列化类</span>
        map.put(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"serializer.class"</span>, <span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"kafka.serializer.StringEncoder"</span>);
        conf.put(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"kafka.broker.properties"</span>, map);
        <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// 配置KafkaBolt生成的topic</span>
        conf.put(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"topic"</span>, <span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"topic2"</span>);

        spoutConfig.scheme = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> SchemeAsMultiScheme(<span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> MessageScheme());
<span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">//        spoutConfig.scheme = new SchemeAsMultiScheme(new StringScheme());</span>

        TopologyBuilder builder = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> TopologyBuilder();
        builder.setSpout(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"kafka-spout"</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> KafkaSpout(spoutConfig), <span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">1</span>);
        builder.setBolt(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"kafka-bolt"</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> SequenceBolt()).shuffleGrouping(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"kafka-spout"</span>);
        builder.setBolt(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"kafka-bolt2"</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> KafkaBolt&lt;String, Integer&gt;()).shuffleGrouping(<span class="hljs-string" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,136,0)">"kafka-bolt"</span>);

        String name = KafkaTopology.class.getSimpleName();
        <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">if</span> (args != <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">null</span> &amp;&amp; args.length &gt; <span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">0</span>) {
            <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">// Nimbus host name passed from command line</span>
            conf.put(Config.NIMBUS_HOST, args[<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">0</span>]);
            conf.setNumWorkers(<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">2</span>);
            StormSubmitter.submitTopology(name, conf, builder.createTopology());
        } <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">else</span> {
            <span class="hljs-comment" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(136,0,0)">//本地模式运行</span>
            conf.setMaxTaskParallelism(<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">3</span>);
            LocalCluster cluster = <span class="hljs-keyword" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,136)">new</span> LocalCluster();
            cluster.submitTopology(name, conf, builder.createTopology());
            Utils.sleep(<span class="hljs-number" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,102,102)">60000</span>);
            cluster.killTopology(name);
            cluster.shutdown();
        }
    }
}</code></pre><ul class="pre-numbering" style="margin:0px; padding:6px 0px 40px; list-style:none; line-height:23.8px; position:absolute; width:50px; background-color:rgb(238,238,238); top:0px; left:0px;
